function getXmlHttpObject(){	
	var xmlHttpRequest;
	//不同的浏览器获取对象xmlhttprequest 对象方法不一样
	if(window.ActiveXObject){		
		xmlHttpRequest=new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");		
	}else{
		xmlHttpRequest=new XMLHttpRequest();
	}
		return xmlHttpRequest;
}

var sign = false;
function doSearchSubmitBJ(t){
    var nowKeywValue = $s_("searchinput_"+t).value;
    $s_("searchinput_"+t).value = nowKeywValue;
    if(ad && nowKeywValue == ad_title && !sign){
        window.open(ad_url);
    }else{
        if(nowKeywValue!="请输入关键字（楼盘名/地名/开发商等）" && nowKeywValue!='' && nowKeywValue!=ad_title){
            myXmlHttpRequest=getXmlHttpObject();
            if(myXmlHttpRequest){
                //创建ajax引擎成功
                var url="/house/ajaxrequest/search_keyword_submit.php";
                var data = 'city='+city+"&keyword="+nowKeywValue;
                myXmlHttpRequest.open("post",url,false);
                myXmlHttpRequest.setRequestHeader("Content-Type","application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=utf-8");
                myXmlHttpRequest.onreadystatechange=function chuli(){
                    //接收数据json
                    if(myXmlHttpRequest.readyState==4){
                        if(myXmlHttpRequest.status==200){
                            var result= myXmlHttpRequest.responseText;
                            var arr  = result.split("^");
                            if(arr[0]==100){
                                window.open(arr[1]);
                                return false;
                            }else{
                                $s_('strNamekeyword_'+t).value=nowKeywValue;
                                $s_("form_newhouse_"+t).submit();
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                myXmlHttpRequest.send(data);
                return false;
            }
        }else{
            $s_('strNamekeyword_'+t).value='';
            $s_("form_newhouse_"+t).submit();
        }
    }
    return true;
}
var value="请输入关键字（楼盘名/地名/开发商等）";
var ad_url="";
var ad_title="";
var ad = false;
function initSearchBox(){
    $.ajax({
        type:"post",
        url:'/house/ajaxrequest/arealist.php?t='+Math.random(),
        data:{type:"advert", pagename: "default_advert"},
        dataType:'json',
        success:function(d){
            if(d){
                ad_title = d.title;
                ad_url = d.linkurl;
                ad = true;
                $("#searchinput_2").val(d.title);
            }else {
                $("#searchinput_2").val(value);
            }
        }
    });
}
$().ready(function(){
    initSearchBox();
    $("#searchinput_2").blur(function(){
        if($(this).val() == "" && ad)
        {
            setTimeout(function(){
                sign = false;
            },200);
            $(this).val(ad_title);
        }
        $(this).css('color','rgb(153, 153, 153)');
    });
    $("#searchinput_2").focus(function() {
        if(ad && $(this).val() == ad_title){
            sign = true;
        }

    });
});

</script>

<script language="javascript">
function adjustFloatNavPos()
{
    var oriNavOffset = $("#orginalNaviBox").offset();
    var oriNavPosition = $("#orginalNaviBox").position();
    var scrTop = $(window).scrollTop();
    var docuTop = scrTop-oriNavOffset.top;  // 当docuTop>=0时，表示导航已不在视野
    if(docuTop >= 0)
    {
		$("#floatNaviBox").show();
    }
    else
    {
		$("#floatNaviBox").hide();
    }
}
$(window).resize(adjustFloatNavPos);
$(window).scroll(adjustFloatNavPos);
$(function() {
   adjustFloatNavPos();
   setInterval(adjustFloatNavPos, 100);
});

function doKey(e){  
	var currKey=0,e=e||event; 
	currKey=e.keyCode||e.which||e.charCode;//支持IE、FF 
	if (currKey == 13) {
	    if($("#floatNaviBox").is(":visible")){
		    doSearchSubmitBJ(2);
		}else{
		    doSearchSubmitBJ(1);
		}
		return false;  
	}  
}
$("#searchinput_1").keydown(function(){doKey();});
$("#strNamekeyword_2").keydown(function(){doKey();});
function oversh(id){
	if(id=="show"){
		$("#ewm").show();
	}else{
		$("#ewm").hide();
	}
}

$('#searchinput_2').keypress(function(e){
	if(e.keyCode == 13) 
	{ 
		doSearchSubmitBJ(2);
	} 
});

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(".Inp_qbk").each(function(){
	$(this).bind("change", function () {
	    var pid = $(this).attr('id');
		var txt = pid.split('_')[1];
		if($(this).val()!=$('#hidden_'+txt).val()){
		    $(this).css("background-color","red");
		}
	});
});
function errorSubmit()
{
	var inputIdArray = new Array('minprice','aveprice','maxprice','sale_telphone','sale_rate','sale_date','fix_status','build_category','address','developer');
	var inputIdLength = inputIdArray.length;
	var allEmpty = true;
	var allSame  = true;
	for(var i=0; i<inputIdLength; i++)
	{
		if($("#txt_"+inputIdArray[i]).val() != "")
		{
			allEmpty = false;
		}
		if($("#txt_"+inputIdArray[i]).val() != $("#hidden_"+inputIdArray[i]).val())
		{
			allSame = false;
		}
	}
	if($("#txt_other").val() != "")
	{
		allEmpty = false;
		allSame  = false;
	}
	if(allEmpty)
	{
		alert('请至少填写一项！')
		return false;
	}
	if(allSame)
	{
		alert('请至少更改一项！')
		return false;
	}
	return true;
}
function postError()
{
	if(errorSubmit() == true)
	{
		document.getElementById('errorForm').action = "/house/web/newhouse_new_info.php?newcode=1617732477";
		document.getElementById('errorForm').submit();
		$('#jiucuoBox').hide();
	}
	else
	{
		return false;
	}
}
$(document).click(function (e) {
    var drag = $("#jiucuoBox"),
        dragel = $("#jiucuoBox")[0],
		linkl = $("#jiucuoLink")[0],
        target = e.target;
    if (linkl !== target && dragel !== target && !$.contains(dragel, target)) {
        drag.hide();
    }
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).click(function (e) {
    var drag = $("#jiucuoBox"),
        dragel = $("#jiucuoBox")[0],
		linkl = $("#jiucuoLink")[0],
        target = e.target;
    if (linkl !== target && dragel !== target && !$.contains(dragel, target)) {
        drag.hide();
    }
});
var navi_tg_cell_default = '请输入手机号';
var navi_tg_name_default = '请输入用户名';
var navi_tg_phonecode_default = '验证码';

var bind_phone = '';
//=====判断是否是通行证+绑定手机号+绑定搜房卡用户
$(document).ready(function() {
	var ajaxUrl = "/house/ajaxrequest/isCorrectMobileUser.php?rand="+Math.random();
	$.ajax({
		type:'get',
		dataType:'json',
		url:ajaxUrl,
		data:'',
		complete:function(){},
		error:function(){},
		success:function(msg){
			//如果用户已经登录
			if(msg.uid) {
				$("input#hide_cell").val(msg.bindMobile);
				bind_phone = msg.bindMobile;

				//初始化表框
				signUpFormInit_2();

				if (msg.bindMobile){
					//隐藏获取手机号验证码的对话框
					$("input#navi_tg_phonecode").parent("li").css("display","none");
				}else {
					//显示获取手机号验证码的对话框
					$("input#navi_tg_phonecode").parent("li").css("display","block");
				}
				
			}else {
				//初始化表框
				signUpFormInit_2();
				
			}
		}
	});
})
//给手机号输入框添加事件
$("input#navi_tg_cell").keyup(function() {
	//是否绑定手机号
	if($("input#navi_tg_cell").val()==bind_phone&&bind_phone!=navi_tg_cell_default&&bind_phone!='') {
		//隐藏获取手机号验证码的对话框
		$("input#navi_tg_phonecode").parent("li").css("display","none");
	}else {
		//显示获取手机号验证码的对话框
		$("input#navi_tg_phonecode").parent("li").css("display","block");
	}
})
//===添加表框的动作事件
$("input#navi_tg_cell").focus(function() {
	//检查是否和默认值相同，如果相同，那么直接清空
	if($("input#navi_tg_cell").val()==navi_tg_cell_default) {
		$("input#navi_tg_cell").val('');
	}
})

$("input#navi_tg_name").focus(function() {
	//检查是否和默认值相同，如果相同，那么直接清空
	if($("input#navi_tg_name").val()==navi_tg_name_default) {
		$("input#navi_tg_name").val('');
	}
})
$("input#navi_tg_phonecode").focus(function() {
	//检查是否和默认值相同，如果相同，那么直接清空
	if($("input#navi_tg_phonecode").val()==navi_tg_phonecode_default) {
		$("input#navi_tg_phonecode").val('');
	}
})
//失去焦点动作
$("input#navi_tg_cell").blur(function() {
	//检查是否为空，如果为空那么直接等于默认值
	if($("input#navi_tg_cell").val()=='') {
		$("input#navi_tg_cell").val(navi_tg_cell_default);
	}
})
$("input#navi_tg_name").blur(function() {
	//检查是否为空，如果为空那么直接等于默认值
	if($("input#navi_tg_name").val()=='') {
		$("input#navi_tg_name").val(navi_tg_name_default);
	}
})
$("input#navi_tg_phonecode").blur(function() {
	//检查是否为空，如果为空那么直接等于默认值
	if($("input#navi_tg_phonecode").val()=='') {
		$("input#navi_tg_phonecode").val(navi_tg_phonecode_default);
	}
})
//===初始化表框
function signUpFormInit_2() {
    if(bind_phone!='') {
        $("input#navi_tg_phonecode").parent("li").css("display","none");
    }else {
        $("input#navi_tg_phonecode").parent("li").css("display","block");
    }
	$("input#navi_tg_cell").val((bind_phone!='')?bind_phone:navi_tg_cell_default);
	$("input#navi_tg_name").val(navi_tg_name_default);
	$("input#navi_tg_phonecode").val(navi_tg_phonecode_default);
}
//===验证码发送函数
var HintNum = 60;

var ClockCodeHint;
    // 手机验证码发送点击动作绑定
    $("#tg_getValCode").click(function(){
        //获取手机号码
        var cellphone = $("#navi_tg_cell").val();
        //如果手机号码为空或者为默认的手机号码那么要提示需要填写???????  kftDefaultMobile
        if(!cellphone || cellphone == navi_tg_cell_default) {
            alert("请填写手机号");
            $("#navi_tg_cell").focus();
            return false;
        }
        var cellnum = /^(13[0-9]|15[0-9]|18[0-9]|14[0-9])[0-9]{8}$/; 
        if(cellphone.match(cellnum) == null||cellphone.length!=11) {
            alert("请填写正确的手机号");
            $("#navi_tg_cell").focus();
            return false;
        }
        var ajaxUrl = "/house/web/mobilecode_send_ajax.php";
        $("#tg_getValCode").attr("disabled", true);
        $.ajax({
            type:'get',
            dataType:'json',
            url:ajaxUrl,
            data:{mobile:cellphone,httptype:'passport'},
            complete:function(){},
            error:function(){alert("验证码发送失败，请重试");$("#tg_getValCode").attr("disabled", false);},
            success:function(msg){
                if(msg.result == 1) {
                    alert("发送成功，如果一分钟内没有收到校验短信，请重试");
                    ValCodeHint();
                } else {
                    alert("验证码发送失败，"+msg.msg);
                    $("#tg_getValCode").attr("disabled", false);
                }
            }
        });
    });


function ValCodeHint() {
    $("#tg_getValCode").val(HintNum+"秒后重新获取");
    ClockCodeHint = setInterval(ClockCodeHintFun, 1000);
}

function ClockCodeHintFun() {
    if(HintNum > 0) {
        HintNum--;
        $("#tg_getValCode").val(HintNum+"秒后重新获取");
    } else {
        clearInterval(ClockCodeHint);
        $("#tg_getValCode").val("重新获取验证码");
        $("#tg_getValCode").attr("disabled", false);
        HintNum = 60;
    }
}

//触发立即报名
$("#tg_submit").click(function() {
	var ajaxUrl = "/house/ajaxrequest/tuangou_baoming.php";
	var cellphone = $("#navi_tg_cell").val();
	var uname = $("#navi_tg_name").val();

	var phonecode = $("#navi_tg_phonecode").val();//手机号验证码
	phonecode = (phonecode==''||phonecode==navi_tg_phonecode_default)?'':$("#navi_tg_phonecode").val();
	var strP=/^\d+$/; 
	var reg = /^1(\d){10}$/; 
	if(uname==''||uname==navi_tg_name_default){
		alert("请输入姓名");
		return false;	   
	}
	if(cellphone=='' && !reg.test(cellphone)||cellphone==navi_tg_cell_default){
		alert("请输入正确的电话号码");
		return false;	   
	}		
    var paramData = 'name='+urlencode(uname)+"&cell="+urlencode(cellphone)+"&phonecode="+urlencode(phonecode)+"&newcode="+newcode;
    $.ajax({
        type:'get',
        dataType:'json',
        url:ajaxUrl,
        data:paramData,
        complete:function(){},
        error:function(){},
        success:function(msg){
            if(msg.result == "0") {
            	bind_phone = msg.bind_mobile;
                // 成功则隐藏当前，显示成功
                $("#navTgBmForm").hide();
                $("#navTgBmHasTel").hide();
                $("#navTgBmSuccess").show();
                tuangouUbCode(cellphone,uname);
            } else if(msg.result == "102") {
                alert(msg.message);
                $("#navi_tg_phonecode").val("");
            } else {
                alert(msg.message);
            }
            
            if(msg.captcha=='pass') {
            	bind_phone = msg.bind_mobile;
            	Xml.Request("/house/esf/getusernewhouse.php", null, doHeadloginuser);
            }
            signUpFormInit_2();
        }
    });
})
</script>

var SunshineCoupons = {
	huxingid : ''
};
(function(){
	// check uri
	var uri = window.location.hash;
	var reg = new RegExp('(token)-(baoming)-([0-9]+)');
	var res =uri.match(reg);
	// parameter verify
	if(res && res[1] == 'token' && res[2] == 'baoming' && res[3]) {
		SunshineCoupons.huxingid = res[3];
		$("#qdds_block").trigger('click');
	}else{
		//
	}
}());

function initQddsUserForm()
{
	var msgRes = qddsData4Newcode;
	if(msgRes.bindinfo.ordertime=='1970年01月01日')
	{
		$("#qdds_form_sucsscontent").html('<p class="f14 cl_666">尊敬的用户你好！</p><p class="f14 cl_666">您已在本楼盘报过名啦。</p>');
	}
	else
	{
		$("#qdds_form_sucsscontent").html('<p class="f14 cl_666">尊敬的用户你好！</p><p class="f14 cl_666">您已于'+msgRes.bindinfo.ordertime+'在本楼盘报过名啦。</p>');
	}		
	$("#qdds_form_uimg").html('<a href="http://www.fang.com/xinfangbang/u/'+msgRes.userinfo.user_id+'.htm" target="_blank"><img src="'+msgRes.userinfo.license_url+'" width="64" height="62"></a>');	
	
	var userxing = '';
	if (msgRes.userinfo.score>=0 && msgRes.userinfo.score<=500)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}
	else if(msgRes.userinfo.score>500 && msgRes.userinfo.score<=1000)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}
	else if(msgRes.userinfo.score>1000 && msgRes.userinfo.score<=2000)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}
	else if(msgRes.userinfo.score>2000 && msgRes.userinfo.score<=3000)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}
	else if(msgRes.userinfo.score>3000)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}																								
	$("#qdds_form_userxing").html('<span style=" /*width:64px;*/ height:24px; line-height:24px; text-align:center; display:inline-block;">专属置业顾问</span><span class="f14">：<a href="http://www.fang.com/xinfangbang/u/'+msgRes.userinfo.user_id+'.htm" target="_blank">'+msgRes.userinfo.realname+'</a></span>'+userxing);

	if(!msgRes.userinfo.isonline)
	{
		$("#qdds_form_zixun").css("background","#bbb");

	{

function initDaojishi()
{
	var msgRes = qddsData4Newcode;
	// 2、初始化时间，并开始计时器*
	$.get("/house/ajaxrequest/daojishi.php", { endtime: msgRes.info.discountEndTime,random:Math.random() },
	function(data){
	  data = parseInt(data);
	  if(data > 0) {
		  showQddsDaoJishi(parseInt(data));
	  } else {
		$("#qdds_block").hide();
	  }
	});	 
}

/*
 * 初始化搜房团提交表单
 * */
function initTuanForm(){
	$("#huodong_form").show();
	if(txdapply)
	{
		$("#huodong_gadstxd_div").show();
		var gadstxd = '<input type="checkbox" check="checked" style="margin-top:2px;" id="huodong_gadstxd_check"><label>'+txdapply+'</label>';
		$("#huodong_gadstxd_div").html(gadstxd);
	}
	// 3个输入框默认文字初始化
    qddsCreateFormInput();
    $("#huodong_form_projname").html("<p>"+qddsData4Newcode.houseinfo['projname']+"</p>");
    // 手机验证码发送点击动作绑定
    $("#huodong_form_getcode").bind('click', getcodeclick);   					
	$("#huodong_form_close").bind('click', closeform);
	qddsCreateFormYxlb();//意向
	$('#huodong_form_baoming').attr("disabled", false);
	$("#huodong_form_baoming").bind('click', function(){
		if(qddsCheckform() === false){
			return false;
		}
		var txdstate = 0;
		if($("#huodong_gadstxd_check").attr("checked") == "checked"){
			txdstate = 1;
		}
		var accode = (!$("#huodong_form_authcode").val() || $("#huodong_form_authcode").val() == huodongDefaultAuthcode) ? "" : $("#huodong_form_authcode").val();
		$("#huodong_form_baoming").attr("disabled", true);
		$.ajax({
			type:'get',
			dataType:'json',
			url:'/house/ajaxrequest/huodongtotal_submit.php',
			data:{newcode:currNewcode,typeid:7,aid:qddsData4Newcode.info['aid'], mobile:$("#huodong_form_mobile").val(), realname:$("#huodong_form_realname").val(), authcode:accode, cid:$("#huodong_form_cid").val(),txdstate:txdstate},
			complete:function(){$("#huodong_form_baoming").attr("disabled", false);},
			error:function(){},
			success:function(msg){
				if (msg.uinfo !== undefined) {
					if(msg.uinfo.uid != "" && msg.uinfo.bindMobile != "") {
						qddsData4Newcode.uinfo.uid = msg.uinfo.uid;
						qddsData4Newcode.uinfo.bindMobile = msg.uinfo.bindMobile;
					}
				}
				if(msg.result == 100) {
					$("#huodong_form").hide(); // 关闭表单
					qddsData4Submit = msg; // 提交结果赋值
					initQddsRes(); // 结果层生成
					$("#huodong_res").show(); // 结果层显示
					qddsLayerShowHide(); // 遮罩层
					huodongtotalUbCode($("#huodong_form_mobile").val(),$("#huodong_form_realname").val(),38);
				} else {
					alert("报名失败，"+msg.msg);
				}
			}
		});
	});
}

/**
 * 初始化提交表单
 **/
function initQddsForm() {
	var msgRes = qddsData4Newcode;
	if(txdapply)
	{
		$("#qdds_txd_div").show();
		var qddstxd = '<input type="checkbox" check="checked" style="margin:3px 3px 0 0;vertical-align:-2px;" id="huodong_qddstxd_check"><label>'+txdapply+'</label>';
		$("#qdds_txd_div").html(qddstxd);
	}
	$("#qdds_form_baoming").attr("disabled", false);
	//选择协议
    $("#qdds_form_checkbox").bind('click', function(){
		if($("#qdds_form_checkbox").attr("checked") == 'checked'){			
			$("#qdds_form_xieyi").hide();
			$("#qdds_form_baoming").attr("disabled", false);
		}else{
			$("#qdds_form_xieyi").show();
			$("#qdds_form_baoming").attr("disabled", "disabled");
		}
    });
    $("#qdds_form_projname").html("<p>"+msgRes.houseinfo['projname']+"</p>");
    $("#qdds_form_close").bind('click', closeform);
    // 3个输入框默认文字初始化
    qddsCreateFormInput();
    
    // 手机验证码发送点击动作绑定
    $("#qdds_form_getcode").bind('click', getcodeclick);
    
    // 立即报名点击动作绑定
    $("#qdds_form_baoming").bind('click', function(){
    	if(qddsCheckform() === false){
			return false;
		}
		var txdstate = 0;
		if($("#huodong_qddstxd_check").attr("checked") == "checked"){
			txdstate = 1;
		}
        $("#qdds_form_baoming").attr("disabled", true);
        var accode = (!$("#qdds_form_authcode").val() || $("#qdds_form_authcode").val() == qddsDefaultAuthcode) ? "" : $("#qdds_form_authcode").val();
        $.ajax({
            type:'get',
            dataType:'json',
            url:'/house/ajaxrequest/qudaodianshang_submit.php',
            data:{
				ztsource:ztsource,
				ztryid:ztryid,
				newcode:currNewcode,
				aid:qddsData4Newcode.info['aid'], 
				mobile:$("#qdds_form_mobile").val(), 
				realname:$("#qdds_form_realname").val(), 
				authcode:accode, 
				taoids:$("#qdds_form_yxlb_taoids").val(),
				txdstate:txdstate,
				random:Math.random(),
				huxingid:SunshineCoupons.huxingid
				},
            complete:function(){$("#qdds_form_baoming").attr("disabled", false);},
            error:function(){},
            success:function(msg){               
                if(msg.result == 100) {
                	if(msg.uinfo.uid != "" && msg.uinfo.bindMobile != "") {
                        qddsData4Newcode.uinfo.uid = msg.uinfo.uid;
                        qddsData4Newcode.uinfo.bindMobile = msg.uinfo.bindMobile;
                    }                   
                    qddsData4Submit = msg; // 提交结果赋值
					if(msg.isoldorder == 1)//旧订单显示之前的页面
					{
						qddsData4Newcode = msg;						
						qddsSmsCf = msg.bindinfo.OrderIdres;
						$("#qdds_form").show();
						$("#qdds_form_bmpage").hide();
						$("#qdds_form_sucss").show();
						$("#qdds_ordermanager").show();
						if(msg.bindinfo.type == 4)//跟置业顾问有关联
						{
							$("#qdds_form_zygw").show();							
						}						
						else
						{
							$("#qdds_form_zygw").hide();
						}
						initQddsForm();
						initQddsUserForm();						
						qddsLayerShowHide(); // 遮罩层
						
					}
					else
					{
						$("#qdds_form").hide(); // 关闭表单
						initQddsRes(); // 结果层生成
						$("#qdds_res").show(); // 结果层显示
						if(msg.bindinfo.type == 4)//跟置业顾问有关联
						{
							newcodeData = msg;
							initQddsUserRes();
							$("#qdds_res_zygw").show(); // 置业顾问显示
							$("#qdds_res_erm").hide();
						}
						else
						{
							$("#qdds_res_zygw").hide();
							$("#qdds_res_erm").show(); // 二维码显示
						}												
						qddsLayerShowHide(); // 遮罩层
						var qddstype_b = 7;
						if(msgRes.isButie == 1)
						{
							qddstype_b = 40;
						}
						huodongtotalUbCode($("#qdds_form_mobile").val(),$("#qdds_form_realname").val(),qddstype_b);
					}
                   
                } else {
                    alert("报名失败，"+msg.msg);
                }
            }
        });
    });
}



function initQddsUserRes()
{
	var msg = newcodeData;	
	$("#qdds_res_uimg").html('<a href="http://www.fang.com/xinfangbang/u/'+msg.userinfo.user_id+'.htm" target="_blank"><img class="ddgz_ps fl" src="'+msg.userinfo.license_url+'" width="64" height="62"></a>');	
	
	var userxing = '';
	if (msg.userinfo.score>=0 && msg.userinfo.score<=500)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}
	else if(msg.userinfo.score>500 && msg.userinfo.score<=1000)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}
	else if(msg.userinfo.score>1000 && msg.userinfo.score<=2000)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}
	else if(msg.userinfo.score>2000 && msg.userinfo.score<=3000)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}
	else if(msg.userinfo.score>3000)
	{
		userxing = '<img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif"><img alt="" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/xinfangbang/front/xing.gif">';
	}
	$("#qdds_res_username").html('<span style=" /*width:64px;*/ height:24px; line-height:24px; text-align:center; display:inline-block;">专属置业顾问</span><span class="f14">：<a class="cl_06c" href="http://www.fang.com/xinfangbang/u/'+msg.userinfo.user_id+'.htm" target="_blank">'+msg.userinfo.realname+'</a></span>'+userxing);
	$("#qdds_res_tele").html('：'+msg.houseinfo.tel400);
	//用户是否在线
	if(!msg.userinfo.isonline)//在线
	{
		$("#qdds_res_zixun").css("background","#bbb");
	}
	$("#qdds_res_zixun").bind('click', function()
	{				
		startChatWith(currNewcode,msg.userinfo.user_id,msg.userinfo.username,msg.userinfo.realname,msg.userinfo.projname,msg.userinfo.city,'0');
		$("#qdds_res").hide();
		qddsLayerShowHide();
	});		
}

/**
 * 渠道电商结果元素生成
 **/
function initQddsRes() 
{
	 var resData = qddsData4Submit;
	 $("#"+qddstype+"_res_close").bind('click', function(){
        $("#"+qddstype+"_res").hide();
        if($("#"+qddstype+"_res").is(":hidden")) {
			$("#qddsLayer").detach();
		}
		clearTimeout(sto);
		//initQdds();
    });
	if (qddstype == 'qdds') {
		//补贴内容
		$("#butietxt").html("");
		if(resData.info.butietxtshow == 1)
		{		
			$("#butietxt").show();
			$("#butietxt").html('<p class="f14"><font color="#ff3333">'+resData.info.BuTieMoney+'元</font>搜房补贴已转入您的搜房账户。您通过搜房置业顾问完成购房签约后，在线申领补贴，即可获得剩余全部搜房补贴。<a href="http://newhouse.fang.com/zt/201409/goufangbutiexieyi.html"><img class="ask_icon" src="http://js.soufunimg.com/zbs/newhouse/images/alf.gif " ></a></p>');
		}
		$("#qdds_res_times").html(resData.nowtime);
		$("#qdds_res_projname").html("<p>"+qddsData4Newcode.houseinfo.projname+"</p>");
		$("#qdds_res_ordermanager").bind('click', function()
		{	
			window.open("http://my.fang.com/MyOrder/GetOrderDetails.html?type=qdlp&group=1&orderno="+resData.channelOrerNo+"&NewCode="+currNewcode+"&Mobile="+resData.uinfo.bindMobile);
		});
	
	} else {
		$("#huodong_res_finish").bind('click', function(){
			window.open("http://my.fang.com/MyOrder/GetOrderDetails.html?type=gg&group=1&orderno="+resData.orderNo);
		});
	    $("#huodong_res_projname").html(qddsData4Newcode.houseinfo.projname);
	    $("#huodong_res_fnum").html("<span>购套房数</span>："+resData.buyCount);
	    $("#huodong_res_tele").html("<span>您的手机</span>："+resData.phone);
	    $("#huodong_res_money").html("￥"+resData.ConditionsMoney);
	    $("#huodong_res_youhui").html(resData.Condition);
	    $("#huodong_res_continue").attr("href", resData.payUrl);
		if(resData.isPush == 1){
			$("#huodong_tuisong").show();
		}else{
			$("#huodong_tuisong").hide();
		}
	}
}

}


/**
 * 渠道电商输入框初始化
 **/
function qddsCreateFormInput() {
    // 默认各种赋值
    if($("#"+qddstype+"_form_realname").val() !== qddsDefaultRealname) {
        $("#"+qddstype+"_form_realname").val(qddsDefaultRealname);
    }
    if($("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").val() !== qddsDefaultMobile) {
        $("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").val(qddsDefaultMobile);
		$("#phone_error").hide();
		$("#phone_right").hide();
    }
    if($("#"+qddstype+"_form_authcode").val() !== qddsDefaultAuthcode) {
        $("#"+qddstype+"_form_authcode").val(qddsDefaultAuthcode);
    }
    if (qddstype == 'qdds') {
	    if($("#qdds_form_getcode").html() !== qddsDefaultGetcode) {
	        $("#qdds_form_getcode").html(qddsDefaultGetcode);
	    }
    } else{
    	if($("#huodong_form_getcode").val() !== qddsDefaultGetcode) {
	        $("#huodong_form_getcode").val(qddsDefaultGetcode);
	    }
    }
    if(qddsData4Newcode.uinfo['bindMobile'] !== '') {
        $("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").val(qddsData4Newcode.uinfo['bindMobile']);
		$("#phone_error").hide();
		$("#phone_right").hide();
    }
    if(qddsData4Newcode.uinfo['bindMobile'] !== '') {
        $("#"+qddstype+"_form_acdiv").hide();
    } else {
        $("#"+qddstype+"_form_acdiv").show();
    }
    // 各种动作绑定
    $("#"+qddstype+"_form_realname").bind('focus', function(){
        if($(this).val() == qddsDefaultRealname) {
            $(this).val("");
        }
		$("#"+qddstype+"_form_realname").css("color","#333333");
    }).bind('blur', function(){
        if($(this).val() == "") {
            $(this).val(qddsDefaultRealname);
			$("#"+qddstype+"_form_realname").css("color","#dadada");
        }		
    });
	//图形验证码文本框默认值
	$("#"+qddstype+"_mf_authcode").bind('focus', function(){
        if($(this).val() == qddsDefaultAuthcodename) {
            $(this).val("");
        }
		$("#"+qddstype+"_mf_authcode").css("color","#333333");
    }).bind('blur', function(){
        if($(this).val() == "") {
            $(this).val(qddsDefaultAuthcodename);
			$("#"+qddstype+"_mf_authcode").css("color","#dadada");
        }		
    });
    $("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").bind('focus', function(){
        if($(this).val() == qddsDefaultMobile) {
            $(this).val("");
        }
		$("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").css("color","#333333");
    }).bind('blur', function(){
		var cellnum = /^(13[0-9]|15[0-9]|18[0-9]|14[0-9])[0-9]{8}$/;
		var cellphone = $(this).val();
		if(cellphone == "") {
            $(this).val(qddsDefaultMobile);
			$("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").css("color","#dadada");
        } else {
			if(cellphone.match(cellnum) == null || cellphone.length != 11) {
				$("#phone_error").show();
				$("#phone_right").hide();
				$("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").focus();				
			} else {
				$("#phone_error").hide();
				$("#phone_right").show();
			}
		}
       
    }).bind('keyup', function(){
        if($(this).val() == qddsData4Newcode.uinfo['bindMobile'] && qddsData4Newcode.uinfo['bindMobile'] !== "") {
            $("#"+qddstype+"_form_acdiv").hide();
        } else {
        	if (qddstype == 'qdds') {
        		$("#qdds_form_bmpage").show();
        		$("#qdds_form_sucss").hide();
        		$("#qdds_ordermanager").hide();
        	}
        	$("#"+qddstype+"_form_acdiv").show();
        }
    });
    $("#"+qddstype+"_form_authcode").bind('focus', function(){
        if($(this).val() == qddsDefaultAuthcode) {
            $(this).val("");
        }
		$("#"+qddstype+"_form_authcode").css("color","#333333");
    }).bind('blur', function(){
        if($(this).val() == "") {
            $(this).val(qddsDefaultAuthcode);
			$("#"+qddstype+"_form_authcode").css("color","#dadada");
        }
    });
}

/**
 * 生成表单中意向列表区块
 **/
function qddsCreateFormYxlb() {
    var clist = qddsData4Newcode.info.ConditionList;
    var len = clist.length;
	$("#huodong_form_youhui").html("");
    for(var i=0; i<len; i++) {
        var oneLi = $("<a id='huodong_form_yxlb_chk_"+clist[i]['ConditionId']+"' money='"+clist[i]['ConditionsMoney']+"'>"+clist[i]['Condition']+"</a>");
        oneLi.appendTo($("#huodong_form_youhui"));
    }
    if(1 == 1) {
        $("#huodong_form_youhui a:first").addClass("cur_a").siblings().removeClass("cur_a");
        $("#huodong_form_cid").val(clist[0]['ConditionId']);
        $("#huodong_form_fee").html("￥"+clist[0]['ConditionsMoney']);
    }
	$("#huodong_form_youhui a").bind('click', function(){
		$(this).addClass("cur_a").siblings().removeClass("cur_a");
        $("#huodong_form_cid").val($(this).attr("id").replace("huodong_form_yxlb_chk_", ""));
        $("#huodong_form_fee").html("￥"+$(this).attr("money"));
	});
}

function qddsCheckform(){
	 if(!$("#"+qddstype+"_form_realname").val() || $("#"+qddstype+"_form_realname").val() == qddsDefaultRealname) {
      alert("请填写购房人");
      $("#"+qddstype+"_form_realname").focus();
      return false;
  }
  var cellphone = $("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").val();
  if(!cellphone || cellphone == qddsDefaultMobile) {
      alert("请填写手机号");
      $("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").focus();
      return false;
  }
  var cellnum = /^(13[0-9]|15[0-9]|18[0-9]|14[0-9])[0-9]{8}$/; 
  if(cellphone.match(cellnum) == null||cellphone.length!=11) {
      alert("请填写正确的手机号");
      $("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").focus();
      return false;
  }
  // 验证码区块隐藏了就不用输入了
  if(!$("#"+qddstype+"_form_acdiv").is(':hidden')) {
      if(!$("#"+qddstype+"_form_authcode").val() || $("#"+qddstype+"_form_authcode").val() == qddsDefaultAuthcode) {
          alert("请填写验证码");
          $("#"+qddstype+"_form_authcode").focus();
          return false;
      }
  }
  if (qddstype == 'huodong') {
	   if(!$("#huodong_form_cid").val()) {
			alert("请选择优惠意向");
			return false;
		}
  }
}
function submitButton()
{
	getcodeclick();
}
function getcodeclick(){
	clearInterval(qddsClockCodeHint);
    var cellphone = $("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").val();
    if(!cellphone || cellphone == qddsDefaultMobile) {
        alert("请填写手机号");
        $("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").focus();
        return false;
    }
    var cellnum = /^(17[0-9]|13[0-9]|15[0-9]|18[0-9]|14[0-9])[0-9]{8}$/; 
    if(cellphone.match(cellnum) == null||cellphone.length!=11) {
        alert("请填写正确的手机号");
        $("#"+qddstype+"_form_mobile").focus();
        return false;
    }
    var ajaxUrl = "/house/web/mobilecode_send_ajax.php";
    $("#"+qddstype+"_form_getcode").attr("disabled", true);
    if (qddstype == 'qdds') {
    	$("#qdds_form_getcode").removeAttr("href");
		var authnum = 3;
    }
	else
	{
		var authnum = 4;
	}
	//图形验证码
	authcode = $("#"+qddstype+"_mf_authcode").val();
	if(authcode == '输入图文验证码获取短信')
	{
		authcode = '';
	}
    $.ajax({
        type:'get',
        dataType:'json',
        url:ajaxUrl,
        data:{mobile:cellphone, httptype:"passport",authcode:authcode,authnum:authnum, yz:1},
        complete:function(){},
        error:function(){
        	alert("验证码发送失败，请重试");
        	$("#"+qddstype+"_form_getcode").attr("disabled", false);
        	if (qddstype == 'qdds') {
        		$("#qdds_form_getcode").attr("href","javascript:void(0)");
        	}
        },
        success:function(msg){
			if(msg.type !== 'undefined' && msg.type == 'yz')
			{
				if(msg.result == '0')
				{
					alert(msg.msg);
					$("#"+qddstype+"_mf_authcode").focus();
				}
				$("#"+qddstype+"_authdiv").show();
				$("#"+qddstype+"_form_getcode").attr("disabled", true);
			}
			else
			{
				if(msg.result == 1) {
					alert("发送成功，如果一分钟内没有收到校验短信，请重试");
					qddsValCodeHint();
				} else {
					alert("验证码发送失败，"+msg.msg);					
					$("#"+qddstype+"_form_getcode").attr("disabled", false);
					if (qddstype == 'qdds') {
						$("#qdds_form_getcode").attr("href","javascript:void(0)");
					}
				}
			}
        }
    });
}

function closeform(){
	$("#"+qddstype+"_form").hide();
	clearTimeout(sto);
	if($("#"+qddstype+"_form").is(":hidden")){
		$("#qddsLayer").detach();
	}
	//initQdds();
}

function qddsValCodeHint() {
	if (qddstype == 'qdds') {
		$("#qdds_form_getcode").html("("+qddsHintNum+"秒)重新获取");
	} else {
		$("#huodong_form_getcode").val("("+qddsHintNum+"秒)重新获取");
	}
    qddsClockCodeHint = setInterval(qddsIntervalfun, 1000);
}

function qddsIntervalfun()
{
    if(qddsHintNum > 0) {
        qddsHintNum--;
        if (qddstype == 'qdds'){
        	$("#qdds_form_getcode").html("("+qddsHintNum+"秒)重新获取");
        } else {
        	$("#huodong_form_getcode").val("("+qddsHintNum+"秒)重新获取");
        }
    } else {
    	clearInterval(qddsClockCodeHint);
    	$("#"+qddstype+"_form_getcode").attr("disabled", false);
        if (qddstype == 'qdds'){
        	$("#qdds_form_getcode").html("重新获取验证码");
        	$("#qdds_form_getcode").attr("href","javascript:void(0)");
        } else {
        	$("#huodong_form_getcode").val("重新获取验证码");
        }
        qddsHintNum = 60;
    }
}

function qddsGetSmsHint() {
    $("#qdds_res_sendtocell").html("重新发送("+qddsSmsHintNum+"S)");
    qddsClockSmsHint = setInterval(qddsClockSmsHintFun, 1000);
}

function qddsClockSmsHintFun() {
    if(qddsSmsHintNum > 0) {
        qddsSmsHintNum--;
        $("#qdds_res_sendtocell").html("重新发送("+qddsSmsHintNum+"S)");
    } else {
        clearInterval(qddsClockSmsHint);
        $("#qdds_res_sendtocell").html("重新获取短信");
        $("#qdds_res_sendtocell").attr("disabled", false);
		 $("#qdds_res_sendtocell").attr("href", "javascript:void(0)");
        qddsSmsHintNum = 60;
    }
}
/**
 * 遮罩层处理
 **/
function qddsLayerShowHide() {
    $("#qddsLayer").detach();
    if( !$("#"+qddstype+"_form").is(":hidden") || !$("#"+qddstype+"_res").is(":hidden") ) {
        var layer = $('<div id="qddsLayer" style="height: 100%; width: 100%; position: fixed; left: 0px; top: 0px; z-index: 10000; opacity: 0.6; filter:Alpha(Opacity=60); background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"></div>');
        layer.appendTo($("body"));
    }
}
function showQddsDaoJishi(ts) {
    var timerun = false;
    var Temp;
    var tempts = ts - 1;
    var startTime = (new Date()).getTime();
    var dateLeft = 0;
    var hourLeft = 0;
    var minuteLeft = 0;
    var secondLeft = 0;
    var dateLeftStr = '';
    var hourLeftStr = '';
    var minuteLeftStr = '';
    var secondLeftStr = '';
    if (ts < 0) {  
        ts = 0;  
        dateLeft = 0;  
        hourLeft = 0;  
        minuteLeft = 0;  
        secondLeft = 0;  
    }  else {  
        dateLeft = parseInt(ts / 86400);
        ts = ts - dateLeft * 86400;
        hourLeft = parseInt(ts / 3600);
        ts = ts - hourLeft * 3600;
        minuteLeft = parseInt(ts / 60);
        secondLeft = ts - minuteLeft * 60;

        dateLeftStr = dateLeft;  
        hourLeftStr = hourLeft;  
        minuteLeftStr = minuteLeft;  
        secondLeftStr = secondLeft;  
    }  
    if (hourLeft < 10)  
        hourLeftStr = '0' + hourLeft;
    if (minuteLeft < 10)  
        minuteLeftStr = '0' + minuteLeft;
    if (secondLeft < 10)  
        secondLeftStr = '0' + secondLeft;
    if(dateLeft > 0) {
        $("#qdds_day_num").html(dateLeft);
    } else {
         $("#qdds_day_num").html(0);
    }
    if(hourLeft > 0) {
        $("#qdds_hour_num").html(hourLeft);
    } else {
        $("#qdds_hour_num").html(0);
    }
    if(minuteLeft > 0) {
        $("#qdds_minu_num").html(minuteLeft); 
    } else {
        $("#qdds_minu_num").html(0);
    }
    if(secondLeft > 0) {
        $("#qdds_sec_num").html(secondLeft); 
    } else {
        $("#qdds_sec_num").html(0); 
    }
    if(dateLeft >0 || hourLeft > 0 || minuteLeft > 0 || secondLeft > 0) {
        timerun = true;
    } else {
        $("#qdds_block").hide();
        timerun = false;
    }
    if (timerun) {
       sto = setTimeout('showQddsDaoJishi( ' + tempts + ') ', 1000);  
    }
}
//图形验证码
function initNewhouseMFImgCode()
{
	document.getElementById('qdds_mf_authimg').src = authcodeDomain+'/house/web/authcode.php?rnd='+Math.random()+'&type=3';
	document.getElementById('huodong_mf_authimg').src = authcodeDomain+'/house/web/authcode.php?rnd='+Math.random()+'&type=4';
}
initNewhouseMFImgCode();	
function getNewhouseMFImgCode(type,num)
{
   document.getElementById(type+'_mf_authimg').src =authcodeDomain+'/house/web/authcode.php?t='+new Date().getTime()+'&type='+num;
   return false;
}

						<script type="text/javascript">
						var calPrice = "7300";
						function calTotalPriceInit(){
						   var area = $("#bs_calarea  option:selected").val();
						   var totalPrice = (area*calPrice)/10000+"万元";
						   $("#cal_total").html(totalPrice);
						}
						calTotalPriceInit();
						$("#bs_calarea").change(function(){ 
							calTotalPriceInit();
						});
						var $cal = function(id){
						   return document.getElementById(id);
						}
						//本息还款的月还款额(参数: 年利率/贷款总额/贷款总月份)
						function getMonthMoney1(lilv, total, month){
							var lilv_month = lilv / 12;//月利率
							return total * lilv_month * Math.pow(1 + lilv_month, month) / ( Math.pow(1 + lilv_month, month) -1 );
						}
						function myround(v, e){
							var t = 1;
							e = Math.round(e);
							for(; e > 0; t *= 10, e--);
							for(; e < 0; t /= 10, e++);
							return Math.round(v * t) / t;
						}
						function ShowLilvNew(month, lt){
								var indexNumSd = getArrayIndexFromYear(month, 1); // 商贷
							   $cal("singlelv").value = myround(lilv_array[lt][1][indexNumSd] * 100, 2);
							   ext_total(document.calc1);
						}
						function getArrayIndexFromYear(year,dkType){
						   var indexNum = 0;
						   if(dkType == 1){
							  if(year == 1) {
								 indexNum = 1;
							  } else if(year > 1 && year <= 3) {
								 indexNum = 3;
							  } else if(year > 3 && year <= 5) {
								 indexNum = 5;
							  } else {
								 indexNum = 10;
							  }
						   } else if(dkType == 2) {
							  if(year > 5) {
								 indexNum = 10;
							  } else {
								 indexNum = 5;
							  }
						   }
						   return indexNum;
						}
						function ext_total(fmobj){
							//var fmobj = document.calc1;
							$("#all_total1").html('');
							$("#month_money1").html('');
							var years = fmobj.calyears_s.value;
							var month = fmobj.calyears_s.value * 12;
							var lilv = fmobj.singlelv.value / 100;//得到利率
							//var lilv = getlilv(fmobj.callilv_s.value, 1, fmobj.calyears_s.value);//得到利率
							//房款总额
							var fangkuan_total = calPrice * fmobj.calarea_s.value;
							//贷款总额
							var daikuan_total = fangkuan_total * (fmobj.calanjie_s.value / 10);
							//首期付款
							var money_first = fangkuan_total - daikuan_total;
						//2.本息还款
							//月均还款
							var month_money1 = getMonthMoney1(lilv, daikuan_total, month);//调用函数计算
							//fmobj.month_money1.innerHTML = Math.round(month_money1 * 100) / 100 + "(元)";
							$("#month_money1").html(Math.round(month_money1 * 100) / 100 + "(元)");
							//还款总额
							var all_total1 = month_money1 * month;
							var all_total1 = Math.round(all_total1) / 10000;
							all_total1 = Math.round(all_total1*100) / 100;
							$("#all_total1").html(all_total1 + "(万元)");
						}
						ext_total(document.calc1);
						</script>

			var pnotices = '';
			function MianFeiPhone(num){
				if(typeof(num)=='undefined'){
					return false;
				}	
				var mf_authcode;
				var mf_phone;
				var mf_cellphone = $('#mf_cellphone').val();
				var mf_telphone = $('#mf_telphone').val();
				var mf_authcode_1 = $('#mf_authcode_1').val();
				var mf_authcode_2 = $('#mf_authcode_2').val();
				if(num==1){
					var reg = /^1[3458][0-9]\d{8}$/;
					if(mf_cellphone=='请输入您的手机号' || mf_cellphone=='')
					{
						alert('请输入手机号码');
						return false;
					}
					else if (!reg.test(mf_cellphone)){
						alert('手机号码格式不正确');
						return false;
					}
					else if(mf_authcode_1==''){
						alert('请输入验证码');
						return false;
					
					} 
					mf_authcode = mf_authcode_1;
					mf_phone = mf_cellphone;
				}
				else if(num==2){
					var reg = /^[0-9]+$/;
					if(mf_telphone=='请输入您的固定电话' || mf_telphone=='')
					{
						alert('请输入电话号码');
						return false;
					}
					else if (!reg.test(mf_telphone)){
						alert('电话号码格式不正确');
						return false;
					}
					else if(mf_authcode_2==''){
						alert('请输入验证码');
						return false;
					}  
					mf_authcode = mf_authcode_2;
					mf_phone = mf_telphone;
				 }	
				
				 $.ajax({ 
					type:"get",
					dataType:'json',		 
					url:"/house/ajaxrequest/callfree.php",
					data:{"telephone":mf_phone,"newcode":newcode,"authcode":mf_authcode},
					complete:function(){},
					error:function(){},
					success:function(result){
						if(result=='正在转接中，请稍候'){
							$('#tc_phone').hide();
							//用户行为函数
							freeCallUbCode(mf_phone);
						}
						alert(result);
					}
				 });
			}

			var isLoginForDy = 0;
			var telephones = '';
			var uid = '';
			<!-- 订阅弹出层弹出 -->
			function cutPriceNotice(type){
				var ajaxUrl = "/house/ajaxrequest/house_subscribe.php";
					$.ajax({
						type:'get',
						dataType:'json',
						url:ajaxUrl,
						data:{isLoginForDy:1},
						complete:function(){},
						success:function(msg){
							if(msg.login == 'yes'){
								isLoginForDy = 1;
								telephones = msg.telephones;
								uid = msg.uid;
								if(isLoginForDy == 1){
									$(".p2").css('display','none');
									$("#tels").val(telephones);
									$('.p1').children('.ti').html("");
									var subscribe = $(".subscribe");
									subscribe.css('display','block');
									subscribeShowHide();
								}
							}else{
								isLoginForDy = 0;
								telephones = msg.telephones;
								uid = msg.uid;
								var subscribe = $(".subscribe");
								subscribe.css('display','block');
								subscribeShowHide();
							}
						}
					});
					
				if(type == 1){
						$('.ml').addClass('lpt_icon');
						$('.mlf').removeClass('lpt_icon');
				}
				if(type == 2){
					$('.mlf').addClass('lpt_icon');
					$('.ml').removeClass('lpt_icon');
				}
			}
			<!-- 关闭订阅弹出层 -->
			function shut(){
				var subscribe = $(".subscribe");
				subscribe.css('display','none');
			
				$("#txdLayer").detach();
					
			}
			
			$(function(){
			//电话
				$("#tels").blur(function(){
					var phone = $("#tels").val();
					if(phone != telephones){
						$(".p2").css('display','block');
						isLoginForDy = 0;
					}
					
					if(!phone || phone == "请输入您的手机号码") {
						alert("请输入您的手机号码");
						$('.p1').children('.ti').html("请输入您的手机号码");
						return false;
					}
					if(phone == telephones){
						$(".p2").css('display','none');
						isLoginForDy = 1;
					}
					var cellphone = $("#tels").val();
					var cellnum = /^(17[0-9]|13[0-9]|15[0-9]|18[0-9]|14[0-9])[0-9]{8}$/; 
					if(cellphone.match(cellnum) == null||cellphone.length!=11) {
						alert("请填写正确的手机号");
						$('.p1').children('.ti').html("请输入您的手机号码");
						$("#tels").val('');
						return false;
					}
					if(phone == ''){
						$('.p1').children('.ti').html("请输入您的手机号码");
					}
				})
				
				$("#tels").focus(function(){
					$('.p1').children('.ti').empty();
				})
				
				//验证码
				$(".code").blur(function(){
					var code = $(".code").val();
					if(code == ''){
						$('.p2').children('.ti').html("请输入验证码");
					}
				})
				$(".code").focus(function(){
					$('.p2').children('.ti').empty();
				})
			})	
			<!-- 提交订阅 -->
			function submits(){
				var phone = $("#tels").val();
				var cellnum = /^(17[0-9]|13[0-9]|15[0-9]|18[0-9]|14[0-9])[0-9]{8}$/; 
				if(phone.match(cellnum) == null||phone.length!=11) {
					alert("请填写正确的手机号");
					$('.p1').children('.ti').html("请输入您的手机号码");
					return false;
				}
				if(phone == ''){
					$('.p1').children('.ti').html("请输入您的手机号码");
					return false;
				}
				var code = $(".code").val();
				if($('.ml').hasClass('lpt_icon')){
					var jjtz = $(".ml").val();
					knotices = 'k';
				}else{
					knotices = '';
				}
				if($('.mlf').hasClass('lpt_icon')){
					var kptz = $(".mlf").val();
					pnotices = 'p';
				}else{
					pnotices = '';
				}
				if(knotices == '' && pnotices == '' ){
					alert('请选择通知类型');
					return false;
				}
				if(isLoginForDy == 0){
					//需要验证验证码(成功直接调订阅接口)
					var ajaxUrl = "/house/ajaxrequest/house_subscribe.php";
					$.ajax({
						type:'get',
						dataType:'json',
						url:ajaxUrl,
						data:{mobile:phone, type: 10,authcode: code,city: city,jjtz:knotices, kptz: pnotices,newcode:currNewcode,types:yzm,projname:projname},
						complete:function(){},
						success:function(msg){
							if(msg.result == 103) {
								alert("手机验证码填写错误！");
								$(".code").val('');
								$('.p2').children('.ti').html("请输入验证码");
								return false;
								//huodongValCodeHintaa();
							}else if(msg.code == 1) {
								$(".subscribe").css('display','none');
								$('.success').css('display','block');
								$('#tip').html('恭喜您，已订阅成功！');
								setTimeout(function(){
									$('.success').css('display','none');document.location.reload();
									},2000);
							}else if(msg.code == 2){
								$(".subscribe").css('display','none');
								$('.success').css('display','block');
								$('#tip').html('您已经订阅过该楼盘了！');
								setTimeout(function(){
									$('.success').css('display','none');document.location.reload();
									},2000);
							}else{
								$(".subscribe").css('display','none');
								$('.success').css('display','block');
								$('#tip').html('由于网络原因添加失败请稍后再试!');
								setTimeout(function(){
									$('.success').css('display','none');document.location.reload();
									},2000);
							}
							
						}
					});
				}else{
					var ajaxUrl = "/house/ajaxrequest/house_subscribe.php";
					$.ajax({
						type:'get',
						dataType:'json',
						url:ajaxUrl,
						data:{mobile:phone, type: 10,authcode: code,city: city,jjtz:knotices, kptz: pnotices,newcode:currNewcode,projname:projname},
						complete:function(){},
						success:function(msg){
							if(msg.code == 1) {
								$(".subscribe").css('display','none');
								$('.success').css('display','block');
								$('#tip').html('恭喜您，已订阅成功！');
								setTimeout(function(){
									$('.success').css('display','none');document.location.reload();
									},2000);
							}else if(msg.code == 2){
								$(".subscribe").css('display','none');
								$('.success').css('display','block');
								$('#tip').html('您已经订阅过该楼盘了！');
								setTimeout(function(){
									$('.success').css('display','none');document.location.reload();
									},2000);
							}else{
								$(".subscribe").css('display','none');
								$('.success').css('display','block');
								$('#tip').html('由于网络原因添加失败请稍后再试!');
								setTimeout(function(){
									$('.success').css('display','none');document.location.reload();
									},2000);
							}
							
						}
					});
				
				}
			}
			
			//发送验证码
			function getcode()
			{
				var cellphone = $("#tels").val();
				if(!cellphone || cellphone == "请输入您的手机号码") {
					alert("请填写手机号");
					$("#tels").focus();
					return false;
				}
				var cellnum = /^(17[0-9]|13[0-9]|15[0-9]|18[0-9]|14[0-9])[0-9]{8}$/; 
				if(cellphone.match(cellnum) == null||cellphone.length!=11) {
					alert("请填写正确的手机号");
					$("#tels").focus();
					return false;
				}
				var ajaxUrl = "/house/web/mobilecode_send_ajax.php";
				$("#getcode").attr("disabled", true);
				$.ajax({
					type:'get',
					dataType:'json',
					url:ajaxUrl,
					data:{mobile:cellphone, httptype:"passport"},
					complete:function(){},
					error:function(){alert("验证码发送失败，请重试");$("#getcode").attr("disabled", false);$("#getcode").attr("href","javascript:void(0)");},
					success:function(msg){
						if(msg.result == 1) {
							alert("发送成功");
							huodongValCodeHintaa();
						} else {
							alert("验证码发送失败，"+msg.msg);	
							huodongValCodeHintaa();															
						}
					}
				});
			}
			
			function huodongValCodeHintaa() {
				$("#getcode").val("("+huodongHintNum+"秒)重新获取");
				huodongClockCodeHintaa = setInterval(huodongIntervalfunkftaa, 1000);
			}
			function huodongIntervalfunkftaa()
			{
				if(huodongHintNum > 0) {
					huodongHintNum--;
					$("#getcode").val("("+huodongHintNum+"秒)重新获取");
				} else {
					clearInterval(huodongClockCodeHintaa);
					$("#getcode").val("重新获取验证码");
					$("#getcode").attr("disabled", false);		
					huodongHintNum = 60;
				}
			}

			function chooseType(type){
				if(type == 1)
				{
					if($('.ml').hasClass('lpt_icon')){
						$('.ml').removeClass('lpt_icon');
					}else{
						$('.ml').addClass('lpt_icon');
					}
					
				}
				if(type == 2)
				{	
					if($('.mlf').hasClass('lpt_icon')){
						$('.mlf').removeClass('lpt_icon');
					}else{
						$('.mlf').addClass('lpt_icon');
					}
				
				}
			}
			function subscribeShowHide() {
					$("#txdLayer").detach();
					if( !$(".subscribe").is(":hidden")) {
						var layer = $('<div id="txdLayer" style="height: 100%; width: 100%; position: fixed; left: 0px; top: 0px; z-index: 10000; opacity: 0.6; filter:Alpha(Opacity=60); background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"></div>');
						layer.appendTo($("body"));
					}
				}

<script language="javascript">

var lbToPos = 0; // 当前第几个顶在最前面
var currentPosi = 0;
var anchorPosi = 0;
var lbTotalNum = $("#imageShowSmall li").length;
var anchorNum = 4;
$("#imageShowBig li")[0].style.display = "block";
function SmallImgSliderTo(ind) {
    // 判断imageShowSmall的第几个顶到第一个的位置上
    ind = (ind < 0) ? 0 : ind;
    ind = (ind > lbTotalNum-1) ? (lbTotalNum-1) : ind;
    if(ind >= lbToPos && ind < lbToPos + anchorNum) {  // 当前显示范围内挪动，则不动
        toPos = lbToPos;
    } else if (ind < lbToPos) {
        toPos = ind;
    } else {
        var maxInd = lbTotalNum - anchorNum;
        if(ind > maxInd) {
            toPos = maxInd;
        } else {
            toPos = ind;
        }
    }
    if(ind !== currentPosi) {
        setLbBigImgShow(ind);
    }
    currentPosi = ind;
    lbToPos = toPos;
    SmallImgSliderMoveto(toPos);
	$("#imageShow ul.imagepoint a").each(function(ind1, Ele1){
		if(ind == ind1) {
			$(this).addClass("hover");
		} else {
			$(this).removeClass("hover");
		}
	});
}
function setLbBigImgShow(ind) {
    $("#imageShowBig li").each(function(index, ele){
        if(ind == index) {
            $(this).show().css("display", "block");
        } else {
            $(this).hide();
        }    
    });
}
function SmallImgSliderMoveto(pos) {
    var wid = parseInt($("#imageShowSmall li").css("width").replace("px", "")) + parseInt($("#imageShowSmall li").css("margin-right").replace("px", ""));
    var toleft = 0 - wid * pos;
    $("#imageShowSmall").animate({left:toleft+'px'}, 200);
    // 设置anchor的位置
    var chazhi = currentPosi - lbToPos;
    var toleft = wid * chazhi;
    $("#imageShowSmallAnchor").animate({left:toleft+'px'}, 200);
}
$("#imageShow ul.imagepoint a").each(function(ind, Ele){
    $(this).click(function(){
        SmallImgSliderTo(ind);
    });
});
$("#imageShowSmall li img").each(function(ind, Ele){
    $(this).click(function(){
        SmallImgSliderTo(ind);
    });
});
$("#imageShowSmallNext").click(function(){
    SmallImgSliderTo(currentPosi+1);
});
$("#imageShowSmallPre").click(function(){
    SmallImgSliderTo(currentPosi-1);
});

   $("[id^='tc_']").hide();
}

function initShoucang(){
    if(isLogin){
		$.ajax({
			type:'get',
			dataType:'json',
			url:"/house/ajaxrequest/house_selected.php",
			data:{newcode:newcode},
			error:function(){},
			success:function(result){
				if(result.result_code==100){
				    $("#selectedId").val(result.select_id);
				    $("#sc_star").addClass("solid");
				}
			}
		});		
	}
}
initShoucang();
function shoucangProcess(){
	if($("#sc_star").hasClass("solid")){
	    if(!isLogin){
			var tmpArr = location.href.split("#");
			$("#shHeadBackurl").val(urlencode(tmpArr[0]));
			showid('showlogindiv');			
		}else{
		   var selectid = $("#selectedId").val();
			$.ajax({
				type:'get',
				dataType:'json',
				url:"/house/ajaxrequest/house_favorite_del.php",
				data:{ selectid: selectid, city: vcity ,name: projn, newcode: newcode },
				error:function(){},
				success:function(delResult){
					if(delResult.delres == 100 && delResult.list.result_code == 100) {
					    $("#selectedId").val('');
					    $("#sc_star").removeClass("solid");
						getHouseFavo();
						//$('#shoucang_tips').text('取消收藏成功').fadeIn();
						//setInterval(function(){$('#shoucang_tips').text('').fadeOut();}, 4000);
						$('#shoucang_link').removeClass('have');
						$('#sc_starmr').text('收藏');
						
					} else {
						//$('#shoucang_tips').text('取消收藏失败').fadeIn();
						//setInterval(function(){$('#shoucang_tips').text('').fadeOut();}, 4000);
					}
				}
			});		
		}
	}else{
	    if(!isLogin){
			var tmpArr = location.href.split("#");
			$("#shHeadBackurl").val(urlencode(tmpArr[0]));
			showid('showlogindiv');			
		}else{	
			$.ajax({
				type:'get',
				dataType:'json',
				url:"/house/ajaxrequest/house_shoucang.php",
				data:{ face: face, name: projn,address: address, price: priceright,city: vcity, pricetype: pricetyperight,parentRefresh: 1, time:new Date().getTime(),newcode:newcode },
				error:function(){},
				success:function(result){
				    if(result.msg=='你已经添加过该房源了' || result.msg =='房源成功添加到选房单啦'){
						//$('#shoucang_tips').text(result.msg).fadeIn();
						if (result.msg =='房源成功添加到选房单啦') {
							$('#shoucang_link').addClass('have');
							$('#sc_starmr').text('已收藏');
						}
						//setInterval(function(){$('#shoucang_tips').text('').fadeOut();}, 4000);
				        initShoucang();
						getHouseFavo();
					}
				}
			});
		}
    }
}

    //initGradeStar(scoretotals);

function initGradeStar()
{
	$.ajax({
		type:'get',
		dataType:'json',
		url:"/house/ajaxrequest/housedetail_score201412.php",
		data:{"city":vcity, "newcode":newcode},
		complete:function(){},
		error:function(){},
		success:function(msgRes){
				var scoretotal = msgRes['total_score'];
				var starcontent = '';
				var scoretotalcontent = '';
				//scoretotal = 0;
				if(scoretotal>0){
					for(var i=1;i<6;i++)
					{
						if(i<=scoretotal) //红星
						{
							starcontent += '<li><a id="xfxq_C03_28" href="'+dpOneLink+'" target="_blank"><img src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/images/xqy201410/red_statr.png" width="16" height="16"></a></li>';                                
						}
						else if(i > scoretotal && i == Math.ceil(scoretotal) ) //半颗星
						{
							starcontent += '<li><a href="'+dpOneLink+'" target="_blank" id="xfxq_C03_28"><img src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/images/xqy201410/red_hlfe_statr.png" width="16" height="16"></a></li>';
						}
						else //灰星
						{
							starcontent += '<li><a id="xfxq_C03_28" href="'+dpOneLink+'" target="_blank"><img src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/images/xqy201410/gray_statr.png" width="16" height="16"></a></li>';
						}
					}
					if (msgRes['total_int'])
						{
							scoretotalcontent += '<span  style="margin-right:5px;">'+msgRes['total_int']+'.';
						}
						else
						{
							scoretotalcontent += '0.';
						}
						scoretotalcontent += msgRes["total_decimal"]+'</span>';
						scoretotalcontent +='<span  id="xfxq_C03_28">(';
						if(typeof(msgRes["number_people"]) == 'undefined')
						{
							msgRes["number_people"] = 0;
						}
						scoretotalcontent += parseInt(msgRes["number_people"])+'条点评)</span>';
				}else{
				//msgRes["number_people"] = 0;
					if(msgRes["number_people"]>0){
						var scoretotalcontent1 = "";
						scoretotalcontent1 +='<a style="margin-top: 0px;margin-left: 10px;line-height: 18px;border: none;padding: 0; color: #333;" class="bf" href="#dianpingmodel" id="xfxq_C03_28">(';
						if(typeof(msgRes["number_people"]) == 'undefined')
						{
							msgRes["number_people"] = 0;
						}
						scoretotalcontent1 += parseInt(msgRes["number_people"])+'条点评)</a>';
						starcontent += '<li style="width:170px;height: 16px;line-height: 16px;">暂无人评分'+ scoretotalcontent1+'</li>';
						
					}else{
						starcontent += '<li style="width:240px;"><a style="margin-top: 0px;line-height: 18px;border: none;padding: 0; color: #333;" class="bf" href="#dianpingmodel" id="xfxq_C03_28">点评获取积分，马上第一个点评吧!</a>';
					}
				}
				$("#scorecontent").html(starcontent);
				$("#scoretotalcontent").html(scoretotalcontent);
			}
		});
    
}
//活动用户行为

function huodongtotalUbCode(telephone,name,type_b)
{
	var b=type_b;
	var p={};
	p['nl'] = currNewcode;
	p['p9'] = telephone;
	p['pe'] = urlencode(name);
	if(b !=null && p != null )
	{
		_ub.collect(b,p);
	}
}
function maima_newcode()
{
	 _ub.collect(13,{'nl':'1617732477'}); 
}

<script language="javascript">
var ask_newcode  = '1617732477';
var asktitle= '卓尔・沈阳客厅';
function search_ask(){
	$('#frm_search').attr('action', "http://www.fang.com/ask/search.aspx");
	if($("#ask_newcode")){
		$("#ask_newcode").remove();
	}
	if($('#asktitle').val() == '关于'+asktitle+'的问题请在此提出' || $('asktitle').val() == 'undefined')
	{
		$('#asktitle').val(asktitle);
	}
	$('#frm_search').submit();
}
function ask_title()
{
	$('#frm_search').attr('action', "http://www.fang.com/ask/Ask_StepTwo.aspx");
	$("#frm_search").prepend("<input type='hidden' id='ask_newcode' name='newcode' value='' />");
	$("#ask_newcode").val(ask_newcode);
	if($('#asktitle').val() == '关于'+asktitle+'的问题请在此提出' || $('asktitle').val() == 'undefined')
	{
		$('#asktitle').val(asktitle);
	}
	$('#frm_search').submit();	
}

<script>

ds_layouttotal = 4;
pos_c = "400,273.5";
function showdong(){
    var l = arguments.length;
    if(l>0){
        var showid = arguments[0];
        for(i=0;i<ds_layouttotal;i++){
            if(i==showid){
                if(document.getElementById("xklist"+showid).style.display=='none'){
                    document.getElementById("xklist"+showid).style.display='';//显示
                    document.getElementById("imgcur"+showid).src='http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/images/navupicon.gif';//显示
                }else{
				    closeIt();			
                    document.getElementById("xklist"+i).style.display='none';
                    document.getElementById("imgcur"+i).src='http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/images/navovericon.gif';//显示
                }
            }else{
			    closeIt();
                document.getElementById("xklist"+i).style.display='none';
                document.getElementById("imgcur"+i).src='http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/images/navovericon.gif';//显示
            }
        }    
    }
}
function showtao(dongid,pindex,tindex,roomname,roomnum){
        for(i=0;i<roomnum;i++){
            if(i==tindex){
                if(document.getElementById("taolist_"+pindex+"_"+tindex).style.display=='none'){
                    document.getElementById("taolist_"+pindex+"_"+tindex).style.display='';//显示
                    document.getElementById("imgurl_"+pindex+"_"+tindex).src='http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/images/cuts.png';//显示
					document.getElementById("stylecolor_"+pindex+"_"+tindex).style.background = '#e8f4ff';
					
                }else{
				    closeIt();			
                    document.getElementById("taolist_"+pindex+"_"+tindex).style.display='none';
                    document.getElementById("imgurl_"+pindex+"_"+tindex).src='http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/images/add_c.png';//显示
					document.getElementById("stylecolor_"+pindex+"_"+tindex).style.background = '';
					
                }
            }else{
			    closeIt();
                document.getElementById("taolist_"+pindex+"_"+i).style.display='none';
                document.getElementById("imgurl_"+pindex+"_"+i).src='http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/images/add_c.png';//显示
				document.getElementById("stylecolor_"+pindex+"_"+i).style.background = '';
            }
        }    

}

<script language="javascript">
var defaultGradeScore = new Array(); 
var gradeTypeList = ["jiaotong", "huanjing", "guihua", "peitao", "kaifashang"]; 
var numList = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
var beginDpRequest = false;
var projname = "卓尔・沈阳客厅";
var dianpingDefault = "点评卓尔・沈阳客厅";
var dianpingNewcode = "1617732477";
var city = "沈阳";
var score_array_total = "3.59";////{$score_array.total_int}.{$score_array.total_decimal}
var dianpingClick = false;
var pingLunLink = "http://shenyangketingze.fang.com/dianping/";
var Link = "http://shenyangketingze.fang.com";
var LinkAdd = "http://shenyangketingze.fang.com";
var k=1;
var imgHtml="";

function getStarByScore(score) {
    if(score == 0) {
        return 0;
    } else if(score >0  && score < 1) {
        return 1;
    } else if(score >= 1 && score < 2) {
        return 2;
    } else if(score >= 2 && score < 3) {
        return 3;
    } else if(score >= 3 && score < 4) {
        return 4;
    } else if(score >= 4 && score <= 5) {
        return 5;
    } else {
        return 0;
    }
}
function iniStar() {
    $.each(gradeTypeList, function(i, field){
        var starNum = getStarByScore(defaultGradeScore[i]);
        if(starNum == 1) {
            $("#gradeStarHint_"+field).html(" "+defaultGradeScore[i]+"&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;");
        } else if(starNum == 2) {
            $("#gradeStarHint_"+field).html(" "+defaultGradeScore[i]+"&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;");
        } else if(starNum == 3) {
            $("#gradeStarHint_"+field).html(" "+defaultGradeScore[i]+"&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;");
        } else if(starNum == 4) {
            $("#gradeStarHint_"+field).html(" "+defaultGradeScore[i]+"&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;");
        } else if(starNum == 5) {
            $("#gradeStarHint_"+field).html(" "+defaultGradeScore[i]+"&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;");
        } else {
            $("#gradeStarHint_"+field).html("0");
        }
		$.each(numList, function(j, fieldN){
            var liId = "gradeStarA_"+field+"_"+fieldN;
            if(fieldN <= defaultGradeScore[i]) {
                $("#"+liId).css("background-position", "0px -21px");
            }
			else if(Math.ceil(defaultGradeScore[i]) == starNum &&  Math.ceil(defaultGradeScore[i]) ==fieldN )
			{
				$("#"+liId).css("background-position", "0px -46px");
			}			
			else {
                $("#"+liId).css("background-position", "0px 0px");
            }
        });
    });
}

function initialGradeStar(newcode, ftlist) {
    $("#gradeStarUl").empty();
    $.each(ftlist, function(i, field){
        $.each(numList, function(j, fieldN){
            var starli = $('<li><a id="gradeStarA_'+field+'_'+fieldN+'">'+fieldN+'</a></li>');
            $("#gradeStarUl").append(starli);
        });
        var starli = $('<li><span class="lpdp_red3" id="gradeStarHint_'+field+'"></span></li>');
        $("#gradeStarUl").append(starli);
    });
    iniStar();
}

function comchk() {
	var m=1;
	var id_s = dianpingNewcode+'|';
	$("input[name='toCompare']").each(function(){ 
		if($(this).attr("checked")){ 
			m++;
			id_s += $(this).val();
			id_s +='|';
		}
	});
	if(m < 1) {
		alert('请至少选择一个楼盘！')
	}else if(m >4) {
		alert('最多只能选择四个楼盘！')
	}else if(id_s) {
		window.open(newhouseDomain+"/house/newhouse/newhouse_compare_house.aspx?str_id="+id_s);
	}
}

function mouse(obj, sType) { 
    var oDiv = document.getElementById(obj); 
    if (sType == 'show') {
		oDiv.style.display = 'block';
		var x=$("#mouse").offset();//2657  470
		$(".wfd").css("top",x.top+16+"px");
		$(".wfd").css("left",x.left+"px");
	 } 
    if (sType == 'hide') { oDiv.style.display = 'none';} 
}

function initDpScore() {
	$.ajax({
		type:'get',
		dataType:'json',
		url:"/house/ajaxrequest/housedetail_score201412.php",
		data:{"city":city, "newcode":dianpingNewcode},
		complete:function(){},
		error:function(){},
		success:function(msgRes){
            var score = msgRes;
				defaultGradeScore[0] = score["jiage_sd"];
				defaultGradeScore[1] = score["diduan_sd"];
				defaultGradeScore[2] = score["jiaotong_sd"];
				defaultGradeScore[3] = score["peitao_sd"];
				defaultGradeScore[4] = score["huanjing_sd"];
			var scoreHtml = "";
			for(k=1;k<6;k++){
				if(k<=score['total_score']){
					imgHtml += '<li><a href="'+pingLunLink+'" target="_blank"><img src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/dianpingnew/lpxqallstar.gif" width="12" height="12"></a></li>';
				}else if(k > score['total_score'] && k == Math.ceil(score['total_score']) ){
					imgHtml += '<li><a href="'+pingLunLink+'" target="_blank"><img src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/dianpingnew/lpxqhrefstar.gif" width="12" height="12"></a></li>';
				}else{
					imgHtml += '<li><a href="'+pingLunLink+'" target="_blank"><img src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/dianpingnew/lpxqhuistar.gif" width="12" height="12"></a></li>';
				}
			}
			
			if(score['total_score'] >0){
				scoreHtml += '<dl><dt class="fl">综合评价<font style="font-size:30px; color:#c00; margin-left:5px; display:inline;">'
				scoreHtml += score["total_int"]+'.</font><font style=" font-size:18px;color:#c00;">'+score["total_decimal"]+'</font><font style=" font-size:14px;color:#666;margin-left:5px; display:inline;">分</font></dt><dd class="fl"><ul class="fl" >'+imgHtml+'</ul><span id="xfxq_C03_25"></span>	</dd></dl>';
				
				scoreHtml += '<div class="clear"></div><a href="'+pingLunLink+'" target="_blank"><div class="lp_inf">价格：<em>'+score["jiage_sd"]+'</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;地段：<em>'+score["diduan_sd"]+'</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;交通：<em>'+score["jiaotong_sd"]+'</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;配套：<em>'+score["peitao_sd"]+'</em>&nbsp;&nbsp;环境：<em>'+score["huanjing_sd"]+'</em></div></a>';
			}else{
				if(score["number_people"]>0){
					scoreHtml += '<dl><dt class="fl" style="margin-top: 5px;">综合评价<font style="font-size:30px; color:#c00; margin-left:5px; display:inline;">'
					scoreHtml += '</font></dt><dd class="fl" style="margin-top: 5px;"><span id="xfxq_C03_25" style="color:#333">暂无人评分</span></dd></dl>';
				}else{
					scoreHtml += '<dl><dd class="fl" style="margin-top: 15px;">点评获取积分，马上第一个点评吧!</dd></dl>';
				}
			}
			var renshuHtml = '<li> <span id="purpleCount">'+parseInt(score["number_people"])+'</span>人</li><li> <span id="redCount">'+parseInt(score["number_people"])+'</span>人</li><li> <span id="yellowCount">'+parseInt(score["number_people"])+'</span>人</li><li> <span id="greenCount">'+parseInt(score["number_people"])+'</span>人</li><li> <span id="blueCount">'+parseInt(score["number_people"])+'</span>人</li>';
			$("#score").html(scoreHtml);
			$("#renshu").html(renshuHtml);
			$("#score").css("display","block");
			initialGradeStar(newcode, gradeTypeList);
		}
	});
}
$(function(){
	initDpScore();
});

function addAgree(tid){
if(!isLogin){
	var tmpArr = location.href.split("#");
			$("#shHeadBackurl").val(urlencode(tmpArr[0]));
			showid('showlogindiv');	
}else{
		if(parseInt(tid)<=0){
			return false;
		}
			$.ajax({
				type:'get',
				dataType:'json',
				url:"/house/ajaxrequest/dianping_agree1.php",
				data:{"newcode":dianpingNewcode,"tid":tid},
				complete:function(){},
				error:function(){},
				success:function(msgRes){
					if(msgRes.code == 100) {
					//alert(msgRes.agree_num);
						var zanHtml = '';
						zanHtml = '<span id="piao_'+tid+'" class="t04 tf">+1</span><a class="t03 mr05" id="agree_'+tid+'" href="javascript:void(0);" title="" onclick="delAgree('+tid+');"><img class="most" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/images/alf.gif" width="12" height="12" /></a>（'+msgRes.agree_num+'）';
						$("#zanbox_"+tid).html(zanHtml);
						$("#piao_"+tid).hide(2000);
					}
					else  {
						alert(msgRes.msg);
					}
				}
			});	
	}
}
function delAgree(tid){
if(!isLogin){
	var tmpArr = location.href.split("#");
	$("#shHeadBackurl").val(urlencode(tmpArr[0]));
	showid('showlogindiv');	
}else{
		if(parseInt(tid)<=0){
			return false;
		}
			$.ajax({
				type:'get',
				dataType:'json',
				url:"/house/ajaxrequest/dianping_agree_del1.php",
				data:{"newcode":dianpingNewcode,"tid":tid},
				complete:function(){},
				error:function(){},
				success:function(msgRes){
					if(msgRes.code == 100) {
					//alert(msgRes.agree_num);
						var zanHtml = '';
						zanHtml = '<span id="piao_'+tid+'" class="t04 tf">-1</span><a class="t033 mr05" id="agree_'+tid+'" href="javascript:void(0);" title="赞" onclick="addAgree('+tid+');"><img class="best" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/images/alf.gif" width="12" height="12" /></a>（'+msgRes.agree_num+'）';
						$("#zanbox_"+tid).html(zanHtml);
						$("#piao_"+tid).hide(2000);
					}
					else{
						alert(msgRes.msg);
					}
				}
			});	
	}
}

<script language="javascript">
function getScrollingPosition( ) {
    var position = [0,0];
    if ( typeof window.pageYOffset != 'undefined') {
       position = [ window.pageXOffset, window.pageYOffset];
    } else if ( typeof document.documentElement.scrollTop != 'undefined' && document.documentElement.scrollTop > 0) {
          position = [ document.documentElement.scrollLeft,document.documentElement.scrollTop];                       
    } else if (typeof document.body.scrollTop != 'undefined') {
          position = [ document.body.scrollLeft , document.body.scrollTop];
    }
    return position;
}
var beginUbRequest = false;
var citySuo = "sy";
function initUbRequest()
{
    _ub.onload=function(){
        var ubDistrict = getN9District(5);
        var ubPrice = _ub.np;
        var ubOperastion = _ub.n5;
        var ubP9 = _ub.values['p9'];
        var requestUrl = "/house/web/ubRequest.php?frompage=xfxq&strDistrict=" + ubDistrict + "&strPrice=" + ubPrice + "&strOperastion=" + ubOperastion + "&exclude=1617732477&getBbs=1&width=174&height=115" + "&time=" + new Date().getTime();
        Xml.Request(requestUrl, null, callback_displayMaylike, null);
        
    };
    _ub.request('n');
}
function getN9District(num)
{
    var returnString = ""; var getNum = 0;
    for(var i=0; i<20; i++)
    {
        var string = _ub.n9;
        if(typeof(string) != 'undefined')
        {
            _ub.load(0);
            var stringArr = string.split("^");
            if(stringArr[2] == '1')
            {
                returnString += stringArr[0]+"|";
                getNum++;
                if(getNum == num)
                {
                    return returnString;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    return returnString;
}
function padLeft(str,len)
{
    str = str.toString();
    if(str.length >= len)
        return str;
    else
        return padLeft("0" +str,len);
} 
function callback_displayMaylike()
{
    var getData = this.responseText;
	//alert(getData);
    if(getData)
    {
        var obj = eval('(' + getData + ')');
        var htmlContent = "";
		var Olgth = obj.length - 1;
		var j=0;
		var strnewcode_p = '';
        for(var i=0; i<obj.length; i++)
        {
        	j=i+1;
        	
        	strnewcode_p = strnewcode_p+','+obj[i]['newcode']+'^'+j+'^'+obj[i]['frompageid'];
            var divIdList = new Array();
			divIdList[0] = "new"+citySuo+"xq_B05_"+padLeft(i*5+1, 2); 
			divIdList[1] = "new"+citySuo+"xq_B05_"+padLeft(i*5+2, 2); 
			divIdList[2] = "new"+citySuo+"xq_B05_"+padLeft(i*5+3, 2); 
			divIdList[3] = "new"+citySuo+"xq_B05_"+padLeft(i*5+4, 2); 
			divIdList[4] = "new"+citySuo+"xq_B05_"+padLeft(i*5+5, 2);
            if(citySuo != 'bj' || citySuo != 'sh'){
				divIdList[0] = '';
				divIdList[1] = '';
				divIdList[2] = '';
				divIdList[3] = '';
				divIdList[4] = '';
				}
            var dis = obj[i]['district'] ? obj[i]['district']+" " : "";
            var pri = parseInt(obj[i]['price']) ? obj[i]['price']+obj[i]['priceUnit'] : "待定";
            var logoPic = '';
			var bbsInfo ='';
            var labels = "<p>"+obj[i]['address']+"</p>";
            if(obj[i]['lab1'] && obj[i]['lab2'])
            {
                labels += "<p><span class='ptlist_tip_1 ts_linear mr05'><a href='"+obj[i]['lab1Link']+"' target='_blank'>"+obj[i]['lab1']+"</a></span><span class='ptlist_tip_2 ts_linear'><a href='"+obj[i]['lab2Link']+"' target='_blank'>"+obj[i]['lab2']+"</a></span></p>";
            }
            if(obj[i]['from'] == 'dingtouad')
            {
                logoPic = '<img class="pa_rt" src="http://img1.soufun.com/house/detail_php/images/housedetail/dtbk_tbtj.png" />';
            }
			if(obj[i]['forumurl'])
			{
			    bbsInfo = "<span class='cl_999 f12' style='width:90px; float:right; text-align:right;'>[<a href='"+obj[i]['forumurl']+"' title='"+obj[i]['projname']+"业主论坛' target='_blank'>论坛</a>]</span>";
			}
			if(i == Olgth){
				var liContent = "<li style='margin-right:0px;'><div class='map_comment'> <div class='dh_c_alone_img'><p><a href='"+obj[i]['imgLink']+"_"+j+"' target='_blank' title='"+dis+obj[i]['projname']+"'><img class='imgts' alt='"+dis+obj[i]['projname']+"' src='"+obj[i]['picture_thumb']+"' border='0'></a></p></div></div><div class='photo_album_txt f14'><span class='photo_album_txt_p' ><a title='' rel='nofollow' href='"+obj[i]['houseurl']+"_"+j+"'  target='_blank'><strong>"+dis+obj[i]['projname']+ "</strong></a></span>"+bbsInfo+"<span style=' width:222px;'>"+pri+"</span><span style=' width:222px;'>"+obj[i]['address']+"</span>"+labels+"</div></li>";
			}else{
				var liContent = "<li><div class='map_comment'> <div class='dh_c_alone_img'><p><a href='"+obj[i]['imgLink']+"_"+j+"' target='_blank' title='"+dis+obj[i]['projname']+"'><img class='imgts' alt='"+dis+obj[i]['projname']+"' src='"+obj[i]['picture_thumb']+"' border='0'></a></p></div>"+logoPic+"</div><div class='photo_album_txt f14'><span class='photo_album_txt_p' ><a title='' rel='nofollow' href='"+obj[i]['houseurl']+"_"+j+"'  target='_blank'><strong>"+dis+obj[i]['projname']+ "</strong></a></span>"+bbsInfo+"<span style=' width:222px;'>"+pri+"</span><span style=' width:222px;'>"+obj[i]['address']+"</span>"+labels+"</div></li>";
			}
			htmlContent += liContent;
        }
        
        strnewcode_p = strnewcode_p.substr(1,10000);
        _ub.collect(1,{'nts':strnewcode_p});
        document.getElementById('divMaylikeUl').innerHTML = htmlContent;
    }
   // document.getElementById('js_jrtabi_0').style.display = '';
	//document.getElementById('js_jrtab_0').style.display = '';
}
window.onscroll = function () {
    var scrollPos = getScrollingPosition();
    if(scrollPos[1] + window.screen.height > parseInt($("#divMaylikePosition").offset().top) && beginUbRequest == false)
    {
        beginUbRequest = true;
        initUbRequest();
    }
	
};
$(function(){
	 $("ul[class='lbtitle'] li").each(function(i){
		$(this).hover(function(){
			$(this).addClass("hover").siblings().removeClass("hover");
			document.getElementById("js_jrtabi_"+i).style.display = '';
			if(i==0){
				$("#js_jrtabi_1").css("display",'none');
				$("#js_jrtabi_2").css("display",'none');
			}else if(i==1){
				$("#js_jrtabi_0").css("display",'none');
				$("#js_jrtabi_2").css("display",'none');
			}else{
				$("#js_jrtabi_0").css("display",'none');
				$("#js_jrtabi_1").css("display",'none');
			}
		});
	 });
});
